<script>
    $(document).ready(function() {//$('#undo').hide();
    });
    var selection = [];
    function Select(id, img) {
        if (selection.indexOf(id) > -1) {
            selection = jQuery.grep(selection, function(value) {
                return value != id;
            });
            $(img).removeClass('img-selected');
            setAction()
            return;
        }
        selection.push(id);
        $(img).addClass('img-selected');
        setAction()
        return false;
    }
    function setAction() {
        if (selection.length > 0) {
            $('#undo').addClass('img-active');
        } else {
            $('#undo').removeClass('img-active');
        }
        if (selection.length > 0) {
            $('#submit').addClass('img-active');
        } else {
            $('#submit').removeClass('img-active');
        }
    }
    function onUndo() {
        selection = [];
        setAction();
        $('.captcha-img').removeClass('img-selected');
    }
    function onReload() {

        ShowLoader();
        window.location.href = window.location.href;
    }
    function ShowLoader() {
        document.getElementById("captcha-global-overlay").style.display = "block";
        return false;
    }
    function onSubmit() {
        if (selection.length <= 0) {
            alert("Invalid selection");
            return false;
        }
        ShowLoader();
        $('#SelectedImages').val(selection.toString());
        $("#captchaForm").submit();

    }
    var onSecuritySubmitSuccess = function(res) {
        if (res.success) {
            HideLoader();
            $('#captcha-message-div').show();
            $('#captcha-main-div').hide();
            window.setTimeout(function() {
                var win = GetMainWindow();
                win.CloseWindow({
                    MethodName: "OnVarifyCaptcha",
                    Prms: res
                });
            }, 500);

            return false;
        } else {
            alert(res.error);
            if (res.exceeded) {
                var win = GetMainWindow();
                win.CloseWindow({
                    MethodName: "OnVarifyCaptcha",
                    Prms: res
                });
                return false;
            }
            window.location.href = window.location.href;
        }
    };
    var onSecuritySubmitComplete = function(res) {};
